 " Chhath Parv or Chhath Puja is a major festival of Hindus celebrated on the Shashthi of Kartik Shukla Paksha
 suryopasna kaa yah mahatvapurn tyohaar karthik maas ke shukla paksh kii chaturthi se saptami tithi tak manaaya jaataa he
 The most important night of this Mahavrat, celebrated a few days after Diwali, is that of Kartik Shukla Shishti, due to which this holy fast and festival was named Chhath
 aasthaa or vishwaas ke saath chaar dinon tak manaaya janevaala yah suryopasna kaa mahaparv bahut hi dhoomdhaam or harshollas ke saath manaaya jaataa he
 This unique folk festival of Suryopasana is mainly celebrated in Bihar, Jharkhand, eastern Uttar Pradesh and Nepal's Terai regions of eastern India
 bihar main to is parv ko rajkeey parv jaisaa darja mila hua he
 Now in the metros like Kolkata, Delhi and Mumbai and its suburbs, the people of Pravasi Bihari and Uttar Pradesh are celebrating this festival in a big way
 yah parv saal main do baar manaaya jaataa he
 First time in Chaitra and second time in Karthik
 caitra shuklapaksh shashthee par manaae jane vaale chhath parv ko chaiti chhath or karthik shukla paksh shashthee par manaae jane vaale parv ko karthik chhath kaha jaataa he
 This festival is celebrated for family happiness and for achieving desired results
 is parv ko stri or purush samaan rup se manaate hai
 The festival of Chhath starts from the sixth day of Deepawali for four days
 in chaaron din shraddhalu bhagwaan surya kii aradhana karke salbhar sukhi, swasth or nirogi hone kii kaamana karte hai
 The four-day Chhath Puja begins on Kartik Shukla Chaturthi and ends on Kartik Shukla Saptami
 is dauraan vratadhari lagaataar chhattis ghante kaa vrath rakhte hai
 During this time they do not even take water
 nahaay khaay- pehla din karthik shukla chaturthi ‚Äònahaay-khaay‚Äô ke rup main manaaya jaataa he
 First of all, the house is cleaned and made clean
 chhath vrati nadiyon ke ghaaton or talabon ke kinare parivaar samet pahunch jate hai tathaa snaan evam puja archana ke saath nahaay-khaay kii rasm ko puraa kiya jaataa he
 After this, Chhathvarthi takes a bath and takes satvik food and starts the fast
 ghar ke sabhi sadsy vrati ke bhojanoparant hi bhojan grahan karte hai
 Pumpkin-lentils and rice are taken as food
 yah daal chane kii hoti he
 Kharna - On the second day, fasting for Kartik Shukla Panchami, fasting throughout the day, they eat in the evening
 ise ‚Äòkharnaa‚Äô kaha jaataa he
 All nearby people are invited to take prasad of Kharna
 prasad ke rup main ganne ke ras main bane hue chaaval kii kheer ke saath doodh, chaaval kaa pittha or ghi chupadi roti banaai jaati he
 Salt and sugar are not used in this
 is dauraan puure ghar kii swatchta kaa vishesh dhyaan rakhaa jaataa he
 Sandhya Arghya - On the third day Kartik Shukla Shashthi is made Chhath Prasad on the day
 prasad ke rup main thekua, jise kuch kshetron main tikri bhi kehete hai, ke alaava chaaval ke laddu, jise ladua bhi kaha jaataa he, banaate hai
 Apart from this, the mold and fruit brought in the form of offering are also included as Chhath Prasad
 shaam ko bans kii tokari (daura) or arghya kaa soup sajaayaa jaataa he
 After this, the person who has taken the fast, along with the family and all the people of the neighborhood, walk towards the ghat to offer the sunset sun
 sabhi chhathvrati nadi kinare ikattha hokar samuhik rup se arghya daan sampann karte hai
 Water and milk are offered to the Sun and the sixth maiya is worshiped with prasad filled soup
 ushaa arghya-chauthe din karthik shukla saptami kii subah udiyamaan surya ko arghya diya jaataa he
 The Vratis regroup where they had offered Arghya on the previous evening
 yahaan par ve log pichley shaam kii gai prakriya ko phir doharaate hai
 In the end, the person who has taken the vow, he completes the fast by drinking a syrup of raw milk and eating some prasad
 puranic or lok kathaenth puja kii parampara or uske mahatv kaa pratipaadan karne vaali anek puranic or lok kathaayen prachlit hai
 According to Ramayana-a belief, Lord Rama and Mother Sita fasted and worshiped Suryadev on Kartik Shukla Shashthi on the day of the establishment of Ramrajya after the victory of Lanka
 saptami ko suryoday ke samay punah anushthan kar suryadev se aashirwad praapt kiya tha
 Mahabharata - According to another belief, Chhath festival started in Mahabharata period
 sabase pehle surya putr karn ne surya dev kii puja shuru kii
 Karna was the supreme devotee of Lord Surya
 vah pratidin ghanton qamar tak pani main khade hokar surya ko arghya detaa
 He became a great warrior by the grace of the Sun
 aaj bhi chhath main arghya daan kii yahi paddati prachlit he
 There is another story related to Chhath festival
 katha ke anusaar jab pandav apana sara rajpaat jue main haar gaye, tab draupadi ne chhath vrath rakhaa
 Then his wishes were fulfilled and the Pandavas got the Rajpat back
 lok parampara ke anusaar surya dev or chhathi maiya kaa sambandh bhai-bahan kaa he
 Surya did the first worship of Lok Matrika Shashthi
 puraana-ek anya katha ke anusaar raja priyavad ko koi santan nahin thi, tab maharishi kashyap ne putr prapti ke liye yajna karakar priyavad kii patni malini ko yagyahuti ke liye banaai gai kheer di
 Due to this effect he was born a son but he was born dead
 priyavad putr ko lekar shamshaan gaye or putr viyog main praan tyaagane lage
 At the same time, the Devasena, the psyche of the Lord, appeared and said that 'I am called Shashthi because of the sixth part of the original tendency of creation
 rajan tum meraa pujan karo tathaa or logon ko bhi prerit karo‚Äô
 The king, with a son's will, fasted the goddess Shashthi and received the son Ratna
 yah puja karthik shukla shashthee ko hui thi
 Social and Cultural Significance The most important aspect of Chhath Puja is its simplicity, purity and public standing
 bhakthi or aadhyatm se paripurna is parv ke liye na vishaal pandalon or bhavy mandiron kii jarurat hoti he, na aishwarya yukt murtiyon kii
 This festival spreads the sweetness of folk life, consisting of bamboo-made soup, baskets, pottery, sugarcane juice, jaggery, rice and wheat offerings, and melodious folk songs
 is vrath ke liye na vishesh dhan kii aavashyaktaa he, na purohit kii or naa hi guru kii
 If needed, it is with the neighborhood, which is easily available for service
 is utsav main kharnaa ke utsav se lekar ardhyadaan tak samaaj kii bhoomika nirantar bani rahati he
 It is a monumental and grand performance of collective deeds performed with service and devotion to the common and poor people, forgetting the difficulties of their daily lives
 chhath parv kii parampara ke peeche vaigyanik rahasy bhi chipa hua he
 Shashthi Tithi is a special astronomical occasion
 us samay surya kii parabegni kirane prithvi kii sataha par saamaanya se adhik maatra main ekatra ho jaati hai
 The ability to protect humans from its potential ill effects lies in this tradition
 chhath parv ko manaane se surya ke parabegni kirnon ke hanikaarak prabhaav se jeevon kii raksha sambhav he
 Astronomical conditions like Chhath reach the sun's ultraviolet rays more than normal on Earth on other days
 aisa samajha jaataa he ki is puja ke dauraan sadhak surya kii or mukh karke arghya detaa he to jal bhoomi par giraata he, tab surya kii kirane us jal dhara ko paar karte samay prism prabhaav se anek prakaar kii kirnon main vikhandit ho jaati hai
 It is believed that these rays have an effect on the seeker's body like para-violet rays, which has a curative effect
 kya he chhath manaane kii paramparachath vrath ek kathin tapasya kii tarah he
 Usually this fast is performed by women but some men also observe this fast
 vrath rakhane vaali mahila ko ‚Äòparavaitin‚Äô bhi kaha jaataa he
 In this fast of four days, the fast is to be fasted
 bhojan ke saath hi sukhad shaiyya kaa bhi tyaag kiya jaataa he
 In the room made for the festival, the night is spent by a vrati with the help of a blanket or sheet on the floor
 is utsav main shaamil hone vaale log nae kapade pahante hai
 But Vratis wear clothes which do not have any type of stitching
 mahilaayein sari or purush dhoti pahanakar chhath karte hai
 Yes, it is worth noting here that after starting Chhath, Chhath festival has to be done for years, until a married woman of the next generation is prepared for it
 ghar main kisi kii mrityu ho jane par yah parv nahin manaaya jaataa he
 It is believed that women who fast on Chhath festival receive son Ratna
 putr kii chahat rakhane vaali or putr kii kushalta ke liye saamaanya taur par mahilaayein yah vrath rakhti hai
 But men also keep this fast with full devotion
 chhath utsav ko lekar aaj bhi kaayam he utsaah kaa maahaulbihar main duubate or ugte surya kii puja karne kii sadiyon puraani parampara aaj bhi kaayam he
 From the very next day of Deepawali, the sound of this mahaparva is heard all over Bihar
 mahilaon main is parv ke prati vishesh prem saaf jhalkata he
 During this Mahaparva, almost every house in Bihar is immersed in the atmosphere of devotion
 paramparaagat dhang se yah parv manaane kii baangi yah he ki muhalle ke tamaam log jinamein yuva, bujurg or mahilaayein bhi shaamil hoti he
 People wash and clean the streets with their hands
 ganga tak janevaali sadakon ko ek baar nahin, balki kai baar dhoyaa jaataa he taaki nange paanv chalane vaale chhath vratiyon ko kisi prakaar kii dikkat kaa saamana na karnaa pade
 On the day of Parna, when the Chhath Vrati ties the bundle of soup, tour, coconut, earthen stove and mango sticks and other pooja materials, they walk towards the river of their region singing barefoot Chhath, then all the people on their way cheerfully Look forward to the service
 chhath vratiyon kii seva or unke liye saaf safai main chaahe amir ho yaa garib, bada ho yaa chota puri shraddha se lage rahete hai
 Now some people make temporary ponds near their residential areas and give water to God Sun by filling them in their waist
 vibhinn mohallon main baqayada chhath seva samiti, chhath puja samiti or anya sanghathan apane kshetron main talab nirmaan kaa kaam karte hai
 In this way, there is a festive atmosphere throughout India throughout the year

 manyata he ki yogini ekadshi kaa vrath (yogini Ekadashi Vrat) karne se vrati ko sabhi paapon se mukti mil jaati he

 a king named Kubera used to rule in a city called Alkapuri of Swargalok
 vah bade hi dharmi raja the or bhagwaan shiv ke upaask the

 bhagwaan shiv ke pujan ke liye hem naamak ek mali phulon kii vyavastha karata tha

 phir usne apane ghar kii raah pakad lee
